<h2 class='a-header--2' id='hl_1'>All NPCs Map</h2>
<table class='a-table ' style=''>
  <tr>
    <td width="100%">・Click on the arrow in the upper left corner to access our sidebar to check all other pins and even search for individual pins.
    <br> ・Pins checked off the map will reflect in the list below.
    <br> ・Use the Regions dropdown menu and the Search Bar to filter the pins by subregion (e.g. Bamboo Abode, Heaven's Pier, etc.).
    <br> ・For map pin suggestions, please list down as much information as you can including reward data or complex acquisition methods.  
    <br> ┣ For images, uploading a <b class='a-bold'>full rectangular screenshot</b> with a resolution of  at least <span class='a-red'>728 x 410 pixels</span> will be highly appreciated.
    <br> ┗ Do not forget to mention which Map Layer you are suggesting a pin for.
    <hr class="a-table__line"> We encourage users to <a class='a-link' href=https://game8.co/users/sign_up?utm_source=game8&utm_medium=link&utm_campaign=mapblurb>sign up</a> and <span class='a-red'>log in</span> to save your progress with the map. </td>
  </tr>
</table>

<p class='a-paragraph'></div></p>
<h2 class='a-header--2' id='hl_3'>How to Succeed in AI Chatbot</h2><h3 class='a-header--3' id='hm_1'>Reset Dialogue When Stuck</h3>
<div class='imageLink js-archive-open-image-modal' data-image-url='https://img.game8.co/4336815/12967bd3b67eee5503815a63a6c6a297.png/original' data-micromodal-trigger='js-archive-open-image-modal' data-archive-url=''><img src='data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7' class='a-img lazy lazy-non-square' alt='Where Winds Meet AI Chat Reset Button' data-src='https://img.game8.co/4336815/12967bd3b67eee5503815a63a6c6a297.png/show' width='728' style='height: 0; padding-bottom: calc(px*410/728); padding-bottom: calc(min(100%,728px)*410/728);' /><span class='imageLink__icon'></span></div>

<p class='a-paragraph'>If your conversation has gone off the rails, or doesn&#39;t end no matter what you say, it&#39;s best to simply <b class='a-bold'>reset and start anew</b> the AI Chatbot from a clean slate by clicking the button with a Refresh icon at the top of the chat box. Instead of trying several methods within one conversation, trying one strategy at a time and refreshing if it doesn&#39;t go anywhere is generally more effective.</p>
<h3 class='a-header--3' id='hm_2'>Return to Login Screen if Combat Begins</h3>
<div class='imageLink js-archive-open-image-modal' data-image-url='https://img.game8.co/4336816/63ea2f9833673cf44219c93dfbb185b4.png/original' data-micromodal-trigger='js-archive-open-image-modal' data-archive-url=''><img src='data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7' class='a-img lazy lazy-non-square' alt='Where Winds Meet Logout to Reset NPCs' data-src='https://img.game8.co/4336816/63ea2f9833673cf44219c93dfbb185b4.png/show' width='728' style='height: 0; padding-bottom: calc(px*407/728); padding-bottom: calc(min(100%,728px)*407/728);' /><span class='imageLink__icon'></span></div>

<p class='a-paragraph'>Sometimes, NPCs will suddenly become violent during AI Chatbot dialogues. When this happens, it&#39;s best to just bail out to the login screen; when you return, the NPC will be found just as they were before the conversation started.</p>

<p class='a-paragraph'>If you accidentally kill a dialogue-capable NPC, our experience has shown that they will respawn, but this has not been heavily tested, so it&#39;s best to simply avoid engaging them in combat.</p>
<h3 class='a-header--3' id='hm_3'>Double-Check the Hint</h3>
<div class='imageLink js-archive-open-image-modal' data-image-url='https://img.game8.co/4336814/061dc290de524c3332142167464fbf7c.png/original' data-micromodal-trigger='js-archive-open-image-modal' data-archive-url=''><img src='data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7' class='a-img lazy lazy-non-square' alt='Where Winds Meet NPC AI Chat Hint' data-src='https://img.game8.co/4336814/061dc290de524c3332142167464fbf7c.png/show' width='728' style='height: 0; padding-bottom: calc(px*410/728); padding-bottom: calc(min(100%,728px)*410/728);' /><span class='imageLink__icon'></span></div>

<p class='a-paragraph'>Even if the NPC appears to be happy with the result of your discussion, this won&#39;t always end the dialogue. Double-checking the text written in the hint will imply the win condition, so try strategies which will lead the dialogue towards that result.</p>
<h2 class='a-header--2' id='hl_4'>What are NPCs in Where Winds Meet?</h2><h3 class='a-header--3' id='hm_4'>NPCs Have AI Integrated Conversations</h3>
<p class='a-paragraph'>Aside from regular NPCs with static dialogue, there will be some NPCs that are integrated with AI generated responses which means that you can <b class='a-bold'>chat with them</b> and have <b class='a-bold'>dynamic responses as a reply</b> to your messages.</p>
<h3 class='a-header--3' id='hm_5'>Befriend NPCs to Gain Rewards</h3>
<figure class='a-figure'><img src='data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7' class='a-img lazy lazy-non-square' alt='NPC Gift' data-src='https://img.game8.co/4337520/58ee6660d097c7d9f89e15943b174933.png/show' width='728' style='height: 0; padding-bottom: calc(px*409/728); padding-bottom: calc(min(100%,728px)*409/728);' /></figure>

<p class='a-paragraph'>Sending NPCs the right responses to their dialogue will raise your relationship rank level with them. At certain relationship thresholds, NPCs might even give you rewards such as <b class='a-bold'>gifts</b>.</p>
